We are in Carlsbad on a business trip from out of state.  I found the address of this shop on line.  I am very pleased to find them.

< Review>
In A Nutshell:

-La Lune Sucree aka The Sweet Moon is a great place to grab some breakfast.
-The little outdoor patio parallel to the Paseo de San Antonio makes for a picture perfect scene reminiscent your favorite "arrondissement" in Paris.
-Now to the food, if you like crepes theres plenty choices here.
-Their avocado toast is delicious along w/ their Breakfast Bendict.
-They also love dogs here & while we were dining they offered to give our dog some chicken..how awesome is that!

Overall, this a nice taste of France right here in DTSJ (Downtown San Jose)!< /Review>

< text>
I visited here for a Saturday brunch. Nice European-style bakery.

PRO: I had Moon over Norway (ham, poached egg, cheese, etc) and the stuff inside the crepe was EXCELLENT. Poached eggs were so good and just the overall flavor was great. Nice patio. Chocolate macaroon (the coconut flake thing, not the colourful mini-burger looking thing) was good. Almont croissant was good... like 7.5~8 out of 10.

CON: The actual crepes. They were hard, rubbery, difficult to cut, and too chewy. I thought they were more like the Chinese scallion pancakes, but even tougher. Service felt a bit on the slow side.

I give it 3 stars plus 1 more star for the excellent crepe filling.<//text>
